          /\n             <a href="/wiki/Angular_velocity" title="Angular velocity">\n              velocity\n             </a>\n            </li>\n           </ul>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td style="padding:0 0.1em 0.4em">\n         <div class="NavFrame collapsed" style="border:none;padding:0">\n          <div class="NavHead" style="font-size:105%;background:transparent;text-align:left;background:#ddf;text-align:center;">\n           Scientists\n          </div>\n          <div class="NavContent plainlist" style="font-size:105%;padding:0.2em 0 0.4em;text-align:center;padding-top:0.35em;">\n           <div class="hlist">\n            <ul>\n             <li>\n              <a href="/wiki/Galileo_Galilei" title="Galileo Galilei">\n               Galileo\n              </a>\n             </li>\n             <li>\n              <a href="/wiki/Isaac_Newton" title="Isaac Newton">\n               Newton\n              </a>\n             </li>\n             <li>\n              <a href="/wiki/Johannes_Kepler" title="Johannes Kepler">\n               Kepler\n              </a>\n             </li>\n             <li>\n              <a href="/wiki/Jeremiah_Horrocks" title="Jeremiah Horrocks">\n               Horrocks\n              </a>\n             </li>\n             <li>\n              <a href="/wiki/Edmond_Halley" title="Edmond Halley">\n               Halley\n              </a>\n             </li>\n             <li>\n              <a href="/wiki/Leonhard_Euler" title="Leonhard Euler">\n               Euler\n              </a>\n             </li>\n             <li>\n              <a href="/wiki/Jean_le_Rond_d%27Alembert" title="Jean le Rond d\'Alembert">\n               d\'Alembert\n              </a>\n             </li>\n             <li>\n              <a href="/wiki/Alexis_Clairaut" title="Alexis Clairaut">\n               Clairaut\n              </a>\n             </li>\n             <li>\n              <a href="/wiki/Joseph-Louis_Lagrange" title="Joseph-Louis Lagrange">\n               Lagrange\n              </a>\n             </li>\n             <li>\n              <a href="/wiki/Pierre-Simon_Laplace" title="Pierre-Simon Laplace">\n               Laplace\n              </a>\n             </li>\n             <li>\n              <a title="Johann Bernoulli">\n               Johann Bernoulli\n              </a>\n             </li>\n             <li>\n              <a href="/wiki/Augustin-Louis_Cauchy" title="Augustin-Louis Cauchy">\n               Cauchy\n              </a>\n             </li>\n            </ul>\n           </div>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td style="text-align:right;font-size:115%;padding-top: 0.6em;padding-top:0.15em;">\n         <div class="plainlinks hlist navbar mini">\n          <ul>\n           <li class="nv-view">\n            <a href="/wiki/Template:Classical_mechanics" title="Template:Classical mechanics">\n             <abbr title="View this template">\n              v\n             </abbr>\n            </a>\n           </li>\n           <li class="nv-talk">\n            <a href="/wiki/Template_talk:Classical_mechanics" title="Template talk:Classical mechanics">\n             <abbr title="Discuss this template">\n              t\n             </abbr>\n            </a>\n           </li>\n           <li class="nv-edit">\n            <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template:Classical_mechanics&amp;action=edit">\n             <abbr title="Edit this template">\n              e\n             </abbr>\n            </a>\n           </li>\n          </ul>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Gyroskop.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="444" data-file-width="282" height="346" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b9/Gyroskop.jpg/220px-Gyroskop.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b9/Gyroskop.jpg 1.5x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Gyroskop.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         This\n         <a href="/wiki/Gyroscope" title="Gyroscope">\n          gyroscope\n         </a>\n         remains upright while spinning due to the conservation of its angular momentum.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Physics" title="Physics">\n        physics\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <b>\n        angular momentum\n       </b>\n       (rarely,\n       <b>\n        moment of momentum\n       </b>\n       or\n       <b>\n        rotational momentum\n       </b>\n       ) is the rotational comparison to\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Linear_momentum" title="Linear momentum">\n        linear momentum\n       </a>\n       . It is an important quantity in physics because it is a\n       <a href="/wiki/Conservation_law" title="Conservation law">\n        conserved quantity\n       </a>\n       \xe2\x80\x93 the angular momentum of a system remains constant unless acted on by an external\n       <a href="/wiki/Torque" title="Torque">\n        torque\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The definition of angular momentum for a\n       <a href="/wiki/Point_particle" title="Point particle">\n        point particle\n       </a>\n       is a\n       <a href="/wiki/Pseudovector" title="Pseudovector">\n        pseudovector\n       </a>\n       <b>\n        r\n       </b>\n       \xc3\x97\n       <b>\n        p\n       </b>\n       , the\n       <a href="/wiki/Cross_product" title="Cross product">\n        cross product\n       </a>\n       of the particle\'s\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Position_vector" title="Position vector">\n        position vector\n       </a>\n       <b>\n        r\n       </b>\n       (relative to some origin) and its\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Momentum_vector" title="Momentum vector">\n        momentum vector\n       </a>\n       <b>\n        p\n       </b>\n       =\n       <i>\n        m\n       </i>\n       <b>\n        v\n       </b>\n       . This definition can be applied to each point in\n       <a href="/wiki/Continuum_mechanics" title="Continuum mechanics">\n        continua\n       </a>\n       like solids or fluids, or\n       <a href="/wiki/Field_(physics)" title="Field (physics)">\n        physical fields\n       </a>\n       . Unlike momentum, angular momentum does depend on where the origin is chosen, since the particle\'s position is measured from it. The angular momentum of an object can also be connected to the\n       <a href="/wiki/Angular_velocity" title="Angular velocity">\n        angular velocity\n       </a>\n       <b>\n        \xcf\x89\n       </b>\n       of the object (how fast it rotates about an axis) via the\n       <a href="/wiki/Moment_of_inertia" title="Moment of inertia">\n        moment of inertia\n       </a>\n       <i>\n        I\n       </i>\n       (which depends on the shape and distribution of mass about the axis of rotation). However, while\n       <b>\n        \xcf\x89\n       </b>\n       always points in the direction of the rotation axis, the angular momentum\n       <b>\n        L\n       </b>\n       may point in a\n       <i>\n        different\n       </i>\n       direction depending on how the mass is distributed.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Angular momentum is additive; the total angular momentum of a system is the (pseudo)\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vector_sum" title="Vector sum">\n        vector sum\n       </a>\n       of the angular momenta. For continua or fields one uses\n       <a href="/wiki/Integral" title="Integral">\n        integration\n       </a>\n       . The total angular momentum of anything can always be split into the sum of two main components: "orbital" angular momentum about an axis outside the object, plus "spin" angular momentum through the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Centre_of_mass" title="Centre of mass">\n        centre of mass\n       </a>\n       of the object.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Torque can be defined as the rate of change of angular momentum, analogous to\n       <a href="/wiki/Force" title="Force">\n        force\n       </a>\n       . The conservation of angular momentum helps explain many observed phenomena, for example the increase in rotational speed of a spinning\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Figure_skater" title="Figure skater">\n        figure skater\n       </a>\n       as the skater\'s arms are contracted, the high rotational rates of\n       <a href="/wiki/Neutron_star" title="Neutron star">\n        neutron stars\n       </a>\n       , the\n       <a href="/wiki/Falling_cat_problem" title="Falling cat problem">\n        falling cat problem\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Precession" title="Precession">\n        precession\n       </a>\n       of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Spinning_top" title="Spinning top">\n        tops\n       </a>\n       and gyros. Applications include the\n       <a href="/wiki/Gyrocompass" title="Gyrocompass">\n        gyrocompass\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Control_moment_gyroscope" title="Control moment gyroscope">\n        control moment gyroscope\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Inertial_navigation_system" title="Inertial navigation system">\n        inertial guidance systems\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Reaction_wheel" title="Reaction wheel">\n        reaction wheels\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Flying_disc" title="Flying disc">\n        flying discs or Frisbees\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Earth%27s_rotation" title="Earth\'s rotation">\n        Earth\'s rotation\n       </a>\n       to name a few. In general, conservation does limit the possible motion of a system, but does not uniquely determine what the exact motion is.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Quantum_mechanics" title="Quantum mechanics">\n        quantum mechanics\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Angular_momentum_operator" title="Angular momentum operator">\n        angular momentum is an operator\n       </a>\n       with quantized eigenvalues. Angular momentum is subject to the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Heisenberg_uncertainty_principle" title="Heisenberg uncertainty principle">\n        Heisenberg uncertainty principle\n       </a>\n       , meaning that only one component can be measured with definite precision; the other two cannot. Also, the "\n       <a href="/wiki/Spin_(physics)" title="Spin (physics)">\n        spin\n       </a>\n       " of\n       <a href="/wiki/Elementary_particle" title="Elementary particle">\n        elementary particles\n       </a>\n       does not correspond to literal spinning motion.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <div class="toc" id="toc">\n       <div class="toctitle">\n        <h2>\n         Contents\n        </h2>\n       </div>\n       <ul>\n </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n       </ul>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Angular_momentum_in_classical_mechanics">\n        Angular momentum in classical mechanics\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Angular_momentum&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Angular momentum in classical mechanics">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Definition">\n        Definition\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Angular_momentum&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Definition">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main articles:\n       <a href="/wiki/Scalar_(physics)" title="Scalar (physics)">\n        Scalar (physics)\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Euclidean_vector" title="Euclidean vector">\n        Euclidean vector\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <h4>\n       <span id="Scalar_\xe2\x80\x94_angular_momentum_in_two_dimensions">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Scalar_.E2.80.94_angular_momentum_in_two_dimensions">\n        Scalar \xe2\x80\x94 angular momentum in two dimensions\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Angular_momentum&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Scalar \xe2\x80\x94 angular momentum in two dimensions">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Ang_mom_2d.png">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="682" data-file-width="698" height="215" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/96/Ang_mom_2d.png/220px-Ang_mom_2d.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/96/Ang_mom_2d.png/330px-Ang_mom_2d.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/96/Ang_mom_2d.png/440px-Ang_mom_2d.png 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Ang_mom_2d.png" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Velocity" title="Velocity">\n          Velocity\n         </a>\n         of the\n         <a href="/wiki/Particle" title="Particle">\n          particle\n         </a>\n         <i>\n          m\n         </i>\n         with respect to the origin\n         <i>\n          O\n         </i>\n         can be resolved into components parallel to (\n         <i>\n          v\n         </i>\n         <sub>\n          //\n         </sub>\n         ) and perpendicular to (\n         <i>\n          v\n         </i>\n         <sub>\n          \xe2\x8a\xa5\n         </sub>\n         ) the radius vector\n         <i>\n          r\n         </i>\n         . The\n         <b>\n          angular momentum\n         </b>\n         of\n         <i>\n          m\n         </i>\n         is proportional to the\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Perpendicular_component" title="Perpendicular component">\n          perpendicular component\n         </a>\n         <i>\n          v\n         </i>\n         <sub>\n          \xe2\x8a\xa5\n         </sub>\n         of the velocity, or equivalently, to the perpendicular distance\n         <i>\n          r\n         </i>\n         <sub>\n          \xe2\x8a\xa5\n         </sub>\n         from the origin.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Angular momentum is a\n       <a href="/wiki/Euclidean_vector" title="Euclidean vector">\n        vector\n       </a>\n       quantity (more precisely, a\n       <a href="/wiki/Pseudovector" title="Pseudovector">\n        pseudovector\n       </a>\n       ) that represents the product of a body\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Moment_of_inertia" title="Moment of inertia">\n        rotational inertia\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Angular_velocity" title="Angular velocity">\n        rotational velocity\n       </a>\n       about a particular axis. In the simple case of revolution of a\n       <a href="/wiki/Particle" title="Particle">\n        particle\n       </a>\n       in a\n       <a href="/wiki/Circle" title="Circle">\n        circle\n       </a>\n       about a center of rotation, the particle remaining always in the same\n       <a href="/wiki/Plane_(geometry)" title="Plane (geometry)">\n        plane\n       </a>\n       and having always the same distance from the center, it is sufficient to discard the\n       <a href="/wiki/Euclidean_vector" title="Euclidean vector">\n        vector\n       </a>\n       nature of angular momentum, and treat it as a\n       <a href="/wiki/Scalar_(mathematics)" title="Scalar (mathematics)">\n        scalar\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Wilson_2-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Wilson-2">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Angular momentum can be considered a rotational analog of\n       <a href="/wiki/Momentum" title="Momentum">\n        linear momentum\n       </a>\n       . Thus, where linear momentum\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <mi>\n              p\n             </mi>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle p}\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="p" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/81eac1e205430d1f40810df36a0edffdc367af36" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-left: -0.079ex; width:1.259ex; height:2.009ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       is proportional to\n       <a href="/wiki/Mass" title="Mass">\n        mass\n       </a>\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <mi>\n              m\n             </mi>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle m}\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="m" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0a07d98bb302f3856cbabc47b2b9016692e3f7bc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.051ex; height:1.676ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Speed" title="Speed">\n        linear speed\n       </a>\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <mi>\n              v\n             </mi>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle v}\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="v" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e07b00e7fc0847fbd16391c778d65bc25c452597" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.138ex; height:1.676ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       ,\n      </p>\n      <dl>\n       <dd>\n        <span class="mwe-math-element">\n         <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n          <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n           <semantics>\n            <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n             <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n              <mi>\n               p\n              </mi>\n              <mo>\n               =\n              </mo>\n              <mi>\n               m\n              </mi>\n              <mi>\n               v\n              </mi>\n              <mo>\n               ,\n              </mo>\n             </mstyle>\n            </mrow>\n            <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n             {\\displaystyle p=mv,}\n            </annotation>\n           </semantics>\n          </math>\n         </span>\n         <img alt="p=mv," aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/eb4b93eb594373b6fa496b126057996eefce3364" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-left: -0.079ex; width:8.214ex; height:2.009ex;"/>\n        </span>\n       </dd>\n      </dl>\n      <p>\n       angular momentum\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <mi>\n              L\n             </mi>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle L}\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="L" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/103168b86f781fe6e9a4a87b8ea1cebe0ad4ede8" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.593ex; height:2.176ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       is proportional to\n       <a href="/wiki/Moment_of_inertia" title="Moment of inertia">\n        moment of inertia\n       </a>\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <mi>\n              I\n             </mi>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle I}\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="I" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/535ea7fc4134a31cbe2251d9d3511374bc41be9f" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.182ex; height:2.176ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Angular_frequency" title="Angular frequency">\n        angular speed\n       </a>\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <mi>\n              \xcf\x89\n              <!-- \xcf\x89 -->\n             </mi>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle \\omega }\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="\\omega " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/48eff443f9de7a985bb94ca3bde20813ea737be8" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.456ex; height:1.676ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Worthington_3-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Worthington-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <dl>\n       <dd>\n        <span class="mwe-math-element">\n         <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n          <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n           <semantics>\n            <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n             <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n              <mi>\n               L\n              </mi>\n              <mo>\n               =\n              </mo>\n              <mi>\n               I\n              </mi>\n              <mi>\n               \xcf\x89\n               <!-- \xcf\x89 -->\n              </mi>\n              <mo>\n               .\n              </mo>\n             </mstyle>\n            </mrow>\n            <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n             {\\displaystyle L=I\\omega .}\n            </annotation>\n           </semantics>\n          </math>\n         </span>\n         <img alt="L=I\\omega ." aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d1ce1597dcef54047a562d9108835bcbd8358d32" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:7.998ex; height:2.176ex;"/>\n        </span>\n       </dd>\n      </dl>\n      <p>\n       Unlike mass, which depends only on amount of matter, moment of inertia is also dependent on the position of the axis of rotation and the shape of the matter. Unlike linear speed, which occurs in a straight line, angular speed occurs about a center of rotation. Therefore, strictly speaking,\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <mi>\n              L\n             </mi>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle L}\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="L" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/103168b86f781fe6e9a4a87b8ea1cebe0ad4ede8" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.593ex; height:2.176ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       should be referred to as the angular momentum\n       <i>\n        relative to that center\n       </i>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Taylor90_4-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Taylor90-4">\n         [4]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Because\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <mi>\n              I\n             </mi>\n             <mo>\n              =\n             </mo>\n             <msup>\n              <mi>\n               r\n              </mi>\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n               <mn>\n                2\n               </mn>\n              </mrow>\n             </msup>\n             <mi>\n              m\n             </mi>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle I=r^{2}m}\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="{\\displaystyle I=r^{2}m}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2ce8ff961fab0cdfe7ac50e8bee6d6ef1ee62347" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:8.463ex; height:2.676ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       for a single particle and\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <mi>\n              \xcf\x89\n              <!-- \xcf\x89 -->\n             </mi>\n             <mo>\n              =\n             </mo>\n             <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n              <mfrac>\n               <mi>\n                v\n               </mi>\n               <mi>\n                r\n               </mi>\n              </mfrac>\n             </mrow>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle \\omega ={\\frac {v}{r}}}\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="\\omega ={\\frac  {v}{r}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/12138afcc600a32b1607606c824d2064900871de" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:6.539ex; height:4.676ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       for circular motion, angular momentum can be expanded,\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <mi>\n              L\n             </mi>\n             <mo>\n              =\n             </mo>\n             <msup>\n              <mi>\n               r\n              </mi>\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n               <mn>\n                2\n               </mn>\n              </mrow>\n             </msup>\n             <mi>\n              m\n             </mi>\n             <mo>\n              \xe2\x8b\x85\n              <!-- \xe2\x8b\x85 -->\n             </mo>\n             <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n              <mfrac>\n               <mi>\n                v\n               </mi>\n               <mi>\n                r\n               </mi>\n              </mfrac>\n             </mrow>\n             <mo>\n              ,\n             </mo>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle L=r^{2}m\\cdot {\\frac {v}{r}},}\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="{\\displaystyle L=r^{2}m\\cdot {\\frac {v}{r}},}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/722877e31dc440b02e3df2b8c874eb991f25e4d0" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:13.195ex; height:4.676ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       and reduced to,\n      </p>\n      <dl>\n       <dd>\n        <span class="mwe-math-element">\n         <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n          <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n           <semantics>\n            <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n             <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n              <mi>\n               L\n              </mi>\n              <mo>\n               =\n              </mo>\n              <mi>\n               r\n              </mi>\n              <mi>\n               m\n              </mi>\n              <mi>\n               v\n              </mi>\n              <mo>\n               ,\n              </mo>\n             </mstyle>\n            </mrow>\n            <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n             {\\displaystyle L=rmv,}\n            </annotation>\n           </semantics>\n          </math>\n         </span>\n         <img alt="{\\displaystyle L=rmv,}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3ce9be937fd731eccda69830a7cf2128deecb0ac" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:9.608ex; height:2.509ex;"/>\n        </span>\n       </dd>\n      </dl>\n      <p>\n       the product of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Radius" title="Radius">\n        radius\n       </a>\n       of rotation\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <mi>\n              r\n             </mi>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle r}\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="r" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0d1ecb613aa2984f0576f70f86650b7c2a132538" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.059ex; height:1.676ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       and the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Linear_momentum" title="Linear momentum">\n        linear momentum\n       </a>\n       of the particle\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <mi>\n              p\n             </mi>\n             <mo>\n              =\n             </mo>\n             <mi>\n              m\n             </mi>\n             <mi>\n              v\n             </mi>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle p=mv}\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="p = mv" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2acbe7154884d4dbe30b9a0b399e43cefd8654c7" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-left: -0.079ex; width:7.557ex; height:2.009ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       , where\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <mi>\n              v\n             </mi>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle v}\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="v" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e07b00e7fc0847fbd16391c778d65bc25c452597" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.138ex; height:1.676ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       in this case is the equivalent\n       <a href="/wiki/Speed" title="Speed">\n        linear (tangential) speed\n       </a>\n       at the radius (\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <mo>\n              =\n             </mo>\n             <mi>\n              r\n             </mi>\n             <mi>\n              \xcf\x89\n              <!-- \xcf\x89 -->\n             </mi>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle =r\\omega }\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="{\\displaystyle =r\\omega }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d6e4dba86b9dc9a24f00a378577b4546dedc376e" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:4.979ex; height:1.676ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       ).\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       This simple analysis can also apply to non-circular motion if only the component of the motion which is\n       <a href="/wiki/Perpendicular" title="Perpendicular">\n        perpendicular\n       </a>\n       to the\n       <a href="/wiki/Position_(vector)" title="Position (vector)">\n        radius vector\n       </a>\n       is considered. In that case,\n      </p>\n      <dl>\n       <dd>\n        <span class="mwe-math-element">\n         <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n          <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n           <semantics>\n            <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n             <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n              <mi>\n               L\n              </mi>\n              <mo>\n               =\n              </mo>\n              <mi>\n               r\n              </mi>\n              <mi>\n               m\n              </mi>\n              <msub>\n               <mi>\n                v\n               </mi>\n               <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                <mo>\n                 \xe2\x8a\xa5\n                 <!-- \xe2\x8a\xa5 -->\n                </mo>\n               </mrow>\n              </msub>\n              <mo>\n               ,\n              </mo>\n             </mstyle>\n            </mrow>\n            <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n             {\\displaystyle L=rmv_{\\perp },}\n            </annotation>\n           </semantics>\n          </math>\n         </span>\n         <img alt="{\\displaystyle L=rmv_{\\perp },}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/54cba40e6e82b32083735501d13f41e68cccf06d" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:11.126ex; height:2.509ex;"/>\n        </span>\n       </dd>\n      </dl>\n      <p>\n       where\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <msub>\n              <mi>\n               v\n              </mi>\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n               <mo>\n                \xe2\x8a\xa5\n                <!-- \xe2\x8a\xa5 -->\n               </mo>\n              </mrow>\n             </msub>\n             <mo>\n              =\n             </mo>\n             <mi>\n              v\n             </mi>\n             <mi>\n              sin\n             </mi>\n             <mo>\n              \xe2\x81\xa1\n              <!-- \xe2\x81\xa1 -->\n             </mo>\n             <mo stretchy="false">\n              (\n             </mo>\n             <mi>\n              \xce\xb8\n              <!-- \xce\xb8 -->\n             </mi>\n             <mo stretchy="false">\n              )\n             </mo>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle v_{\\perp }=v\\sin(\\theta )}\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="{\\displaystyle v_{\\perp }=v\\sin(\\theta )}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/163f5f644793a0f6eb62286bb838848317b0a8cb" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:13.108ex; height:2.843ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       is the perpendicular component of the motion. Expanding,\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <mi>\n              L\n             </mi>\n             <mo>\n              =\n             </mo>\n             <mi>\n              r\n             </mi>\n             <mi>\n              m\n             </mi>\n             <mi>\n              v\n             </mi>\n             <mi>\n              sin\n             </mi>\n             <mo>\n              \xe2\x81\xa1\n              <!-- \xe2\x81\xa1 -->\n             </mo>\n             <mo stretchy="false">\n              (\n             </mo>\n             <mi>\n              \xce\xb8\n              <!-- \xce\xb8 -->\n             </mi>\n             <mo stretchy="false">\n              )\n             </mo>\n             <mo>\n              ,\n             </mo>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle L=rmv\\sin(\\theta ),}\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="{\\displaystyle L=rmv\\sin(\\theta ),}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f093a6fdb253e9d684af3f225239b92697cba364" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:15.813ex; height:2.843ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       rearranging,\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <mi>\n              L\n             </mi>\n             <mo>\n              =\n             </mo>\n             <mi>\n              r\n             </mi>\n             <mi>\n              sin\n             </mi>\n             <mo>\n              \xe2\x81\xa1\n              <!-- \xe2\x81\xa1 -->\n             </mo>\n             <mo stretchy="false">\n              (\n             </mo>\n             <mi>\n              \xce\xb8\n              <!-- \xce\xb8 -->\n             </mi>\n             <mo stretchy="false">\n              )\n             </mo>\n             <mi>\n              m\n             </mi>\n             <mi>\n              v\n             </mi>\n             <mo>\n              ,\n             </mo>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle L=r\\sin(\\theta )mv,}\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="{\\displaystyle L=r\\sin(\\theta )mv,}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e0e238548108c2e9e0c3ea696da8500c9885015c" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:15.813ex; height:2.843ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       and reducing, angular momentum can also be expressed,\n      </p>\n      <dl>\n       <dd>\n        <span class="mwe-math-element">\n         <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n          <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n           <semantics>\n            <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n             <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n              <mi>\n               L\n              </mi>\n              <mo>\n               =\n              </mo>\n              <msub>\n               <mi>\n                r\n               </mi>\n               <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                <mo>\n                 \xe2\x8a\xa5\n                 <!-- \xe2\x8a\xa5 -->\n                </mo>\n               </mrow>\n              </msub>\n              <mi>\n               m\n              </mi>\n              <mi>\n               v\n              </mi>\n              <mo>\n               ,\n              </mo>\n             </mstyle>\n            </mrow>\n            <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n             {\\displaystyle L=r_{\\perp }mv,}\n            </annotation>\n           </semantics>\n          </math>\n         </span>\n         <img alt="{\\displaystyle L=r_{\\perp }mv,}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/eb8528a226fa2915919bed41269ad720065d1352" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:11.126ex; height:2.509ex;"/>\n        </span>\n       </dd>\n      </dl>\n      <p>\n       where\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <msub>\n              <mi>\n               r\n              </mi>\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n               <mo>\n                \xe2\x8a\xa5\n                <!-- \xe2\x8a\xa5 -->\n               </mo>\n              </mrow>\n             </msub>\n             <mo>\n              =\n             </mo>\n             <mi>\n              r\n             </mi>\n             <mi>\n              sin\n             </mi>\n             <mo>\n              \xe2\x81\xa1\n              <!-- \xe2\x81\xa1 -->\n             </mo>\n             <mo stretchy="false">\n              (\n             </mo>\n             <mi>\n              \xce\xb8\n              <!-- \xce\xb8 -->\n             </mi>\n             <mo stretchy="false">\n              )\n             </mo>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle r_{\\perp }=r\\sin(\\theta )}\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="{\\displaystyle r_{\\perp }=r\\sin(\\theta )}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9e429dae54c4064967213f2be1cf6170f814e664" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:12.95ex; height:2.843ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       is the length of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Torque#Moment_arm_formula" title="Torque">\n        <i>\n         moment arm\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       , a line dropped perpendicularly from the origin onto the path of the particle. It is this definition,\n       <span class="texhtml">\n        (length of moment arm)\xc3\x97(linear momentum)\n       </span>\n       to which the term\n       <i>\n        moment of momentum\n       </i>\n       refers.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Dadourian_5-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Dadourian-5">\n         [5]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span id="Scalar_\xe2\x80\x94_angular_momentum_from_Lagrangian_mechanics">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Scalar_.E2.80.94_angular_momentum_from_Lagrangian_mechanics">\n <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       Another approach is to define angular momentum as the conjugate momentum of the angular coordinate\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <mi>\n expressed in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Lagrangian_mechanics" title="Lagrangian mechanics">\n        Lagrangian\n       </a>\n       of the mechanical system. Consider a mechanical system with a mass\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <mi>\n              m\n             </mi>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle m}\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="m" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0a07d98bb302f3856cbabc47b2b9016692e3f7bc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.051ex; height:1.676ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       constrained to move in a circle of radius\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <mi>\n              a\n             </mi>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle a}\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.24ex; height:1.676ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       in the absence of any external force field.        </b>\n         ), and angular momentum (\n         <b>\n          L\n         </b>\n         ) vectors in a rotating system. (r) is the radius.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       To completely define angular momentum in\n       <a href="/wiki/Three-dimensional_space" title="Three-dimensional space">\n        three dimensions\n       </a>\n       , it is required to know the\n       <a href="/wiki/Angular_velocity" title="Angular velocity">\n        angle swept out in unit time\n       </a>\n       , the direction of the axis of rotation, and the sense (right- or left-handed) of the rotation, as well as the\n       <a href="/wiki/Mass" title="Mass">\n        mass\n       </a>\n       involved.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6">\n        <a href="#cite_note-6">\n         [6]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By retaining this\n       <a href="/wiki/Euclidean_vector" title="Euclidean vector">\n        vector\n       </a>\n       nature of angular momentum, the general nature of the equations is also retained, and can describe any sort of three-dimensional\n       <a href="/wiki/Motion_(physics)" title="Motion (physics)">\n        motion\n       </a>\n       about the center of rotation \xe2\x80\x93\n       <a href="/wiki/Circular_motion" title="Circular motion">\n        circular\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Linear_motion" title="Linear motion">\n        linear\n       </a>\n       , or otherwise. In\n       <a href="/wiki/Vector_notation" title="Vector notation">\n        vector notation\n       </a>\n       , the angular momentum of a\n       <a href="/wiki/Point_particle" title="Point particle">\n        particle\n       </a>\n       in motion about the\n       <a href="/wiki/Origin_(mathematics)" title="Origin (mathematics)">\n        origin of coordinates\n       </a>\n       is src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a271a96e7b925fd39686375167c76d406e87c813" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:8.077ex; height:2.009ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       of the particle. By the definition of the cross product, the\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n              <mi mathvariant="bold">\n               L\n              </mi>\n             </mrow>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle \\mathbf {L} }\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="\\mathbf {L} " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6f5f750865376a1a4ae2b15a00b4ff9c75a66630" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.619ex; height:2.176ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       vector is\n       <a href="/wiki/Perpendicular" title="Perpendicular">\n        perpendicular\n       </a>\n       to both\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n              <mi mathvariant="bold">\n               r\n              </mi>\n             </mrow>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle \\mathbf {r} }\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="\\mathbf {r} " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/eca0f46511c4c986c48b254073732c0bd98ae0c1" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.113ex; height:1.676ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       and\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n              <mi mathvariant="bold">\n               p\n              </mi>\n             </mrow>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle \\mathbf {p} }\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="\\mathbf {p} " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/dd73e3862cb92b016721b8c492eadb4e8a577527" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.496ex; height:2.009ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       . It is directed along the axis of rotation as indicated by the\n       <a href="/wiki/Right-hand_rule" title="Right-hand rule">\n        right-hand rule\n       </a>\n       \xe2\x80\x93 so that the rotation is seen as\n       <a href="/wiki/Clockwise" title="Clockwise">\n        counter-clockwise\n       </a>\n       from the head of the vector. Conversely, the\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n          <semantics>\n           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n             <mrow aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6f5f750865376a1a4ae2b15a00b4ff9c75a66630" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.619ex; height:2.176ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       vector defines the\n       <a href="/wiki/Plane_(geometry)" title="Plane (geometry)">\n        plane\n       </a>\n       in which\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n results, where\n      </p>\n      <dl>\n       <dd>\n        <span class="mwe-math-element">\n         <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n    </mi>\n             <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n               <mover>\n                <mi mathvariant="bold">\n                 u\n </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="\\mathbf {L} =rmv\\mathbf {\\hat {u}} " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0a761fad402cde98517baffffd37adae166f765d" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:10.472ex; height:2.343ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       for circular motion, where all of the motion is perpendicular to the radius\n       <span class="mwe-math-element">\n        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display:      <mi>\n              r\n             </mi>\n            </mstyle>\n           </mrow>\n           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n            {\\displaystyle r}\n           </annotation>\n          </semantics>\n         </math>\n        </span>\n        <img alt="r" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0d1ecb613aa2984f0576f70f86650b7c2a132538" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.059ex; height:1.676ex;"/>\n       </span>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Discussion">\n        Discussion\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Angular_momentum&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Discussion">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Angular momentum can be described as the rotational analog of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Linear_momentum" title="Linear momentum">\n        linear momentum\n       </a>\n       . Like linear momentum it involves elements of\n       <a href="/wiki/Mass" title="Mass">\n        mass\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Displacement_(vector)" title="Displacement (vector)">\n        displacement\n       </a>\n       . Unlike linear momentum it also involves elements of\n       <a href="/wiki/Position_(vector)" title="Position (vector)">\n        position\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Shape" title="Shape">\n        shape\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Many problems in physics involve matter in motion about some certain point in space, be it in actual rotation about it, or simply moving past it, where it is desired to know what effect the moving matter has on the point \xe2\x80\x94 can it exert energy upon it or perform work about it?\n       <a href="/wiki/Energy" title="Energy">\n        Energy\n       </a>\n       , the ability to do\n       <a href="/wiki/Work_(physics)" title="Work (physics)">\n        work\n       </a>\n       , can be stored in matter by setting it in motion \xe2\x80\x94 a combination of its\n       <a href="/wiki/Inertia" title="Inertia">\n        inertia\n       </a>\n       and its displacement. Inertia is measured by its\n       <a href="/wiki/Mass" title="Mass">\n        mass\n       </a>\n       , and displacement by its\n       <a href="/wiki/Velocity" title="Velocity">\n        velocity\n       </a>\n       . Their product,\n      </p>\n      <dl>\n       <dd>\n        <span class="mwe-math-element">\n         <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n          <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n           <semantics>\n            <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n             <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n               <mtable columnalign="right left right left right left right left right left right left" columnspacing="0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em" displaystyle="true" rowspacing="3pt">\n                <mtr>\n                 <mtd>\n                  <mo stretchy="false">\n                   (\n                  </mo>\n                  <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                   <mtext>\n                    amount of inertia\n                   </mtext>\n                  </mrow>\n                  <mo stretchy="false">\n                   )\n                  </mo>\n                  <mo>\n                   \xc3\x97\n                   <!-- \xc3\x97 -->\n                  </mo>\n                  <mo stretchy="false">\n                   (\n                  </mo>\n                  <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                   <mtext>\n                    amount of displacement\n                   </mtext>\n                  </mrow>\n                  <mo stretchy="false">\n                   )\n                  </mo>\n                 </mtd>\n                 <mtd>\n                  <mi>\n                  </mi>\n                  <mo>\n                   =\n                  </mo>\n                  <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                   <mtext>\n                    amount of (inertia\xc2\xb7displacement)\n                   </mtext>\n                  </mrow>\n                 </mtd>\n                </mtr>\n                <mtr>\n                 <mtd>\n              <!-- \xc3\x97 -->\n                  </mo>\n                  <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                   <mtext>\n                    velocity\n                   </mtext>\n       <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                   <mtext>\n                    momentum\n                   </mtext>\n                  </mrow>\n                 </mtd>\n      </mi>\n                  <mo>\n                   =\n                  </mo>\n                  <mi>\n                   p\n                  </mi>\n                 </mtd>\n {\\begin{aligned}({\\text{amount of inertia}})\\times ({\\text{amount of displacement}})&amp;={\\text{amount of (inertia\xc2\xb7displacement)}}\\\\{\\text{mass}}\\times {\\text{velocity}}&amp;={\\text{momentum}}\\\\m\\times v&amp;=p\\\\\\end{aligned}}}\n            </annotation>\n           </semantics>\n          </math>\n         </span>\n         <img alt="{\\begin{aligned}({\\text{amount of inertia}})\\times ({\\text{amount of displacement}})&amp;={\\text{amount of (inertia\xc2\xb7displacement)}}\\\\{\\text{mass}}\\times </dd>\n      </dl>\n      <p>\n       is the matter\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Momentum" title="Momentum">\n        momentum\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7">\n        <a href="#cite_note-7">\n         [7]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Referring this momentum to a central point introduces a complication: the momentum is not applied to the point directly. For instance, a particle of matter at the outer edge of a wheel is, in effect, at the end of a\n       <a href="/wiki/Lever" title="Lever">\n        lever\n       </a>\n       of the same length as the wheel\'s radius, its momentum turning the lever about the center point. This imaginary lever is known as the\n       <i>\n        moment arm\n       </i>\n       . It has the effect of multiplying the momentum\'s effort in proportion to its length, an effect known as a\n       <a href="/wiki/Moment_(physics)" title="Moment (physics)">\n        <i>\n         moment\n        </i>\n        .\n       </a>\n       Hence, the particle\'s momentum referred to a particular point,\n      </p>\n      <dl>\n       <dd>\n        <span class="mwe-math-element">\n         <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">\n          <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n           <semantics>\n            <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n             <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n               <mtable columnalign="right left right left right left right left right left right left" columnspacing="0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em" displaystyle="true" rowspacing="3pt">\n                <mtr>\n                 <mtd>\n                  <mo stretchy="false">\n                   (\n                  </mo>\n                  <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                   <mtext>\n                    moment arm\n                   </mtext>\n                  </mrow>\n                  <mo stretchy="false">\n                   )\n                  </mo>\n                  <mo>\n                   \xc3\x97\n                   <!-- \xc3\x97 -->\n                  </mo>\n                  <mo stretchy="false">\n                   (\n                  </mo>\n                  <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                   <mtext>\n                    amount of inertia\n                   </mtext>\n                  </mrow>\n                  <mo stretchy="false">\n                   )\n                  </mo>\n                  <mo>\n                   \xc3\x97\n                   <!-- \xc3\x97 -->\n                  </mo>\n                  <mo stretchy="false">\n                   (\n                  </mo>\n                  <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                   <mtext>\n                    amount of displacement\n                   </mtext>\n                  </mrow>\n                  <mo stretchy="false">\n                   )\n                  </mo>\n                 </mtd>\n                 <mtd>\n                  <mi>\n                  </mi>\n                  <mo>\n                   =\n                  </mo>\n                  <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                   <mtext>\n                    moment of (inertia\xc2\xb7displacement)\n  <mtext>\n                    length\n                   </mtext>\n                  </mrow>\n                  <mo>\n                   \xc3\x97\n                   <!-- \xc3\x97 -->\n                  </mo>\n                  <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                   <mtext>\n                    mass\n                   </mtext>\n                  </mrow>\n                  <mo>\n                   \xc3\x97\n                   <!-- \xc3\x97 -->\n                  </mo>\n                  <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                   <mtext>\n                    velocity\n         </mo>\n                  <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                   <mtext>\n                    moment of momentum\n                   </mtext>\n                  </mrow>\n                 </mtd>\n                </mtr>\n                <mtr>\n                 <mtd>\n                  <mi>\n                   r\n                  </mi>\n                  <mo>\n                <!-- \xc3\x97 -->\n                  </mo>\n                  <mi>\n                   v\n                  </mi>\n                 </mtd>\n                 <mtd>\n                  <mi>\n                  </mi>\n                  <mo>\n                   =\n                  </mo>\n                  <mi>\n                   L\n                  </mi>\n                 </mtd>\n                </mtr>\n               </mtable>\n              </mrow>\n             </mstyle>\n            </mrow>\n            <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\n             {\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}({\\text{moment arm}})\\times ({\\text{amount of inertia}})\\times ({\\text{amount of displacement}})&amp;={\\text{moment of (inertia\xc2\xb7displacement)}}\\\\{\\text{length}}\\times {\\text{mass}}\\times {\\text{velocity}}&amp;={\\text{moment of momentum}}\\\\r\\times m\\times v&amp;=L\\\\\\end{aligned}}}\n            </annotation>\n           </semantics>\n          </math>\n
